# Voice Library

Murf offers an extensive library of voices. Start by selecting your base language and accent. Supported Voices & Languages vary by modelâ€” [Gen2](/api/docs/text-to-speech-models/gen-2) and [Falcon](/api/docs/text-to-speech-models/falcon) each have their own availability. Please refer to the relevant **Model** section (Gen2 or Falcon) for the up-to-date list before choosing a voice. Each voice will have the following details:

* **Voice ID**: The unique identifier for the voice
* **Supported Locale**: the locales other than the base language that the voice supports using [Multilingual technology](/api/docs/text-to-speech/speech-customization#multinative)
* **Voice Styles**: The different styles available for the voice
* **Sample audio**: A sample audio file for the voice

You can copy the Voice ID of a voice and use it in the [Synthesize Speech](/api/docs/api-reference/text-to-speech/generate)Â operation.
